24 /** Space logic for checking exhaustivity and unreachability of pattern matching
25  *
26  *  Space can be thought of as a set of possible values. A type or a pattern
27  *  both refer to spaces. The space of a type is the values that inhabit the
28  *  type. The space of a pattern is the values that can be covered by the
29  *  pattern.
30  *
31  *  Space is recursively defined as follows:
32  *
33  *      1. `Empty` is a space
34  *      2. For a type T, `Typ(T)` is a space
35  *      3. A union of spaces `S1 | S2 | ...` is a space
36  *      4. `Prod(S1, S2, ..., Sn)` is a product space.
37  *
38  *  For the problem of exhaustivity check, its formulation in terms of space is as follows:
39  *
40  *      Is the space Typ(T) a subspace of the union of space covered by all the patterns?
41  *
42  *  The problem of unreachable patterns can be formulated as follows:
43  *
44  *      Is the space covered by a pattern a subspace of the space covered by previous patterns?
45  *
46  *  Assumption:
47  *    (1) One case class cannot be inherited directly or indirectly by another
48  *        case class.
49  *    (2) Inheritance of a case class cannot be well handled by the algorithm.
50  *
51  */
52 
53 
54 /** space definition */
55 sealed trait Space
56 
57 /** Empty space */
58 case object Empty extends Space
59 
60 /** Space representing the set of all values of a type
61  *
62  * @param tp: the type this space represents
63  * @param decomposed: does the space result from decomposition? Used for pretty print
64  *
65  */
66 case class Typ(tp: Type, decomposed: Boolean) extends Space
67 
68 /** Space representing an extractor pattern */
69 case class Prod(tp: Type, unappTp: Type, unappSym: Symbol, params: List[Space], full: Boolean) extends Space
70 
71 /** Union of spaces */
72 case class Or(spaces: List[Space]) extends Space
73 
74 /** abstract space logic */
75 trait SpaceLogic {
76   /** Is `tp1` a subtype of `tp2`? */
77   def isSubType(tp1: Type, tp2: Type): Boolean
78 
79   /** Is `tp1` the same type as `tp2`? */
80   def isEqualType(tp1: Type, tp2: Type): Boolean
81 
82   /** Return a space containing the values of both types.
83    *
84    * The types should be atomic (non-decomposable) and unrelated (neither
85    * should be a subtype of the other).
86    */
87   def intersectUnrelatedAtomicTypes(tp1: Type, tp2: Type): Space
88 
89   /** Is the type `tp` decomposable? i.e. all values of the type can be covered
90    *  by its decomposed types.
91    *
92    * Abstract sealed class, OrType, Boolean and Java enums can be decomposed.
93    */
94   def canDecompose(tp: Type): Boolean
95 
96   /** Return term parameter types of the extractor `unapp` */
97   def signature(unapp: Type, unappSym: Symbol, argLen: Int): List[Type]
98 
99   /** Get components of decomposable types */
100   def decompose(tp: Type): List[Space]
101 
102   /** Display space in string format */
103   def show(sp: Space): String
104 
105   /** Simplify space using the laws, there's no nested union after simplify
106    *
107    *  @param aggressive if true and OR space has less than 5 components, `simplify` will
108    *                    collapse `sp1 | sp2` to `sp1` if `sp2` is a subspace of `sp1`.
109    *
110    *                    This reduces noise in counterexamples.
111    */
112   def simplify(space: Space, aggressive: Boolean = false): Space = space match {
113     case Prod(tp, fun, sym, spaces, full) =>
114       val sp = Prod(tp, fun, sym, spaces.map(simplify(_)), full)
115       if (sp.params.contains(Empty)) Empty
116       else sp
117     case Or(spaces) =>
118       val set = spaces.map(simplify(_)).flatMap {
119         case Or(ss) => ss
120         case s => Seq(s)
121       } filter (_ != Empty)
122 
123       if (set.isEmpty) Empty
124       else if (set.size == 1) set.toList(0)
125       else if (aggressive && spaces.size < 5) {
126         val res = set.map(sp => (sp, set.filter(_ ne sp))).find {
127           case (sp, sps) =>
128             isSubspace(sp, Or(sps))
129         }
130         if (res.isEmpty) Or(set)
131         else simplify(Or(res.get._2), aggressive)
132       }
133       else Or(set)
134     case Typ(tp, _) =>
135       if (canDecompose(tp) && decompose(tp).isEmpty) Empty
136       else space
137     case _ => space
138   }
139 
140   /** Flatten space to get rid of `Or` for pretty print */
141   def flatten(space: Space): List[Space] = space match {
142     case Prod(tp, fun, sym, spaces, full) =>
143       spaces.map(flatten) match {
144         case Nil => Prod(tp, fun, sym, Nil, full) :: Nil
145         case ss  =>
146           ss.foldLeft(List[Prod]()) { (acc, flat) =>
147             if (acc.isEmpty) flat.map(s => Prod(tp, fun, sym, s :: Nil, full))
148             else for (Prod(tp, fun, sym, ss, full) <- acc; s <- flat) yield Prod(tp, fun, sym, ss :+ s, full)
149           }
150       }
151     case Or(spaces) =>
152       spaces.flatMap(flatten _)
153     case _ => List(space)
154   }
155 
156   /** Is `a` a subspace of `b`? Equivalent to `a - b == Empty`, but faster */
157   def isSubspace(a: Space, b: Space): Boolean = {
158     def tryDecompose1(tp: Type) = canDecompose(tp) && isSubspace(Or(decompose(tp)), b)
159     def tryDecompose2(tp: Type) = canDecompose(tp) && isSubspace(a, Or(decompose(tp)))
160 
161     val res = (simplify(a), b) match {
162       case (Empty, _) => true
163       case (_, Empty) => false
164       case (Or(ss), _) =>
165         ss.forall(isSubspace(_, b))
166       case (Typ(tp1, _), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
167         isSubType(tp1, tp2)
168       case (Typ(tp1, _), Or(ss)) =>  // optimization: don't go to subtraction too early
169         ss.exists(isSubspace(a, _)) || tryDecompose1(tp1)
170       case (_, Or(_)) =>
171         simplify(minus(a, b)) == Empty
172       case (Prod(tp1, _, _, _, _), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
173         isSubType(tp1, tp2)
174       case (Typ(tp1, _), Prod(tp2, fun, sym, ss, full)) =>
175         // approximation: a type can never be fully matched by a partial extractor
176         full && isSubType(tp1, tp2) && isSubspace(Prod(tp2, fun, sym, signature(fun, sym, ss.length).map(Typ(_, false)), full), b)
177       case (Prod(_, fun1, sym1, ss1, _), Prod(_, fun2, sym2, ss2, _)) =>
178         sym1 == sym2 && isEqualType(fun1, fun2) && ss1.zip(ss2).forall((isSubspace _).tupled)
179     }
180 
181     debug.println(s"${show(a)} < ${show(b)} = $res")
182 
183     res
184   }
185 
186   /** Intersection of two spaces  */
187   def intersect(a: Space, b: Space): Space = {
188     def tryDecompose1(tp: Type) = intersect(Or(decompose(tp)), b)
189     def tryDecompose2(tp: Type) = intersect(a, Or(decompose(tp)))
190 
191     val res: Space = (a, b) match {
192       case (Empty, _) | (_, Empty) => Empty
193       case (_, Or(ss)) => Or(ss.map(intersect(a, _)).filterConserve(_ ne Empty))
194       case (Or(ss), _) => Or(ss.map(intersect(_, b)).filterConserve(_ ne Empty))
195       case (Typ(tp1, _), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
196         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) a
197         else if (isSubType(tp2, tp1)) b
198         else if (canDecompose(tp1)) tryDecompose1(tp1)
199         else if (canDecompose(tp2)) tryDecompose2(tp2)
200         else intersectUnrelatedAtomicTypes(tp1, tp2)
201       case (Typ(tp1, _), Prod(tp2, fun, _, ss, true)) =>
202         if (isSubType(tp2, tp1)) b
203         else if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) a // problematic corner case: inheriting a case class
204         else if (canDecompose(tp1)) tryDecompose1(tp1)
205         else Empty
206       case (Typ(tp1, _), Prod(tp2, _, _, _, false)) =>
207         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2) || isSubType(tp2, tp1)) b  // prefer extractor space for better approximation
208         else if (canDecompose(tp1)) tryDecompose1(tp1)
209         else Empty
210       case (Prod(tp1, fun, _, ss, true), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
211         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) a
212         else if (isSubType(tp2, tp1)) a  // problematic corner case: inheriting a case class
213         else if (canDecompose(tp2)) tryDecompose2(tp2)
214         else Empty
215       case (Prod(tp1, _, _, _, false), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
216         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2) || isSubType(tp2, tp1)) a
217         else if (canDecompose(tp2)) tryDecompose2(tp2)
218         else Empty
219       case (Prod(tp1, fun1, sym1, ss1, full), Prod(tp2, fun2, sym2, ss2, _)) =>
220         if (sym1 != sym2 || !isEqualType(fun1, fun2)) Empty
221         else if (ss1.zip(ss2).exists(p => simplify(intersect(p._1, p._2)) == Empty)) Empty
222         else Prod(tp1, fun1, sym1, ss1.zip(ss2).map((intersect _).tupled), full)
223     }
224 
225     debug.println(s"${show(a)} & ${show(b)} = ${show(res)}")
226 
227     res
228   }
229 
230   /** The space of a not covered by b */
231   def minus(a: Space, b: Space): Space = {
232     def tryDecompose1(tp: Type) = minus(Or(decompose(tp)), b)
233     def tryDecompose2(tp: Type) = minus(a, Or(decompose(tp)))
234 
235     val res = (a, b) match {
236       case (Empty, _) => Empty
237       case (_, Empty) => a
238       case (Typ(tp1, _), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
239         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) Empty
240         else if (canDecompose(tp1)) tryDecompose1(tp1)
241         else if (canDecompose(tp2)) tryDecompose2(tp2)
242         else a
243       case (Typ(tp1, _), Prod(tp2, fun, sym, ss, true)) =>
244         // rationale: every instance of `tp1` is covered by `tp2(_)`
245         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) minus(Prod(tp2, fun, sym, signature(fun, sym, ss.length).map(Typ(_, false)), true), b)
246         else if (canDecompose(tp1)) tryDecompose1(tp1)
247         else a
248       case (_, Or(ss)) =>
249         ss.foldLeft(a)(minus)
250       case (Or(ss), _) =>
251         Or(ss.map(minus(_, b)))
252       case (Prod(tp1, fun, _, ss, true), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
253         // uncovered corner case: tp2 :< tp1
254         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) Empty
255         else if (simplify(a) == Empty) Empty
256         else if (canDecompose(tp2)) tryDecompose2(tp2)
257         else a
258       case (Prod(tp1, _, _, _, false), Typ(tp2, _)) =>
259         if (isSubType(tp1, tp2)) Empty
260         else a
261       case (Typ(tp1, _), Prod(tp2, _, _, _, false)) =>
262         a  // approximation
263       case (Prod(tp1, fun1, sym1, ss1, full), Prod(tp2, fun2, sym2, ss2, _)) =>
264         if (sym1 != sym2 || !isEqualType(fun1, fun2)) a
265         else if (ss1.zip(ss2).exists(p => simplify(intersect(p._1, p._2)) == Empty)) a
266         else if (ss1.zip(ss2).forall((isSubspace _).tupled)) Empty
267         else
268           // `(_, _, _) - (Some, None, _)` becomes `(None, _, _) | (_, Some, _) | (_, _, Empty)`
269           Or(ss1.zip(ss2).map((minus _).tupled).zip(0 to ss2.length - 1).map {
270             case (ri, i) => Prod(tp1, fun1, sym1, ss1.updated(i, ri), full)
271           })
272 
273     }
274 
275     debug.println(s"${show(a)} - ${show(b)} = ${show(res)}")
276 
277     res
278   }
279 }
280 
281 /** Scala implementation of space logic */
282 class SpaceEngine(implicit ctx: Context) extends SpaceLogic {
283   import tpd._
284 
285   private val scalaSomeClass       = ctx.requiredClass("scala.Some")
286   private val scalaSeqFactoryClass = ctx.requiredClass("scala.collection.generic.SeqFactory")
287   private val scalaListType        = ctx.requiredClassRef("scala.collection.immutable.List")
288   private val scalaNilType         = ctx.requiredModuleRef("scala.collection.immutable.Nil")
289   private val scalaConsType        = ctx.requiredClassRef("scala.collection.immutable.::")
290 
291   override def intersectUnrelatedAtomicTypes(tp1: Type, tp2: Type) = {
292     val and = AndType(tp1, tp2)
293     // Precondition: !(tp1 <:< tp2) && !(tp2 <:< tp1)
294     // Then, no leaf of the and-type tree `and` is a subtype of `and`.
295     val res = inhabited(and)
296 
297     debug.println(s"atomic intersection: ${and.show} = ${res}")
298 
299     if (res) Typ(and, true) else Empty
300   }
301 
302   /* Whether the extractor is irrefutable */
303   def irrefutable(unapp: Tree): Boolean = {
304     // TODO: optionless patmat
305     unapp.tpe.widen.finalResultType.isRef(scalaSomeClass) ||
306       (unapp.symbol.is(Synthetic) && unapp.symbol.owner.linkedClass.is(Case)) ||
307       productArity(unapp.tpe.widen.finalResultType) > 0
308   }
309 
310   /** Return the space that represents the pattern `pat`
311    */
312   def project(pat: Tree): Space = pat match {
313     case Literal(c) =>
314       if (c.value.isInstanceOf[Symbol])
315         Typ(c.value.asInstanceOf[Symbol].termRef, false)
316       else
317         Typ(ConstantType(c), false)
318     case _: BackquotedIdent => Typ(pat.tpe, false)
319     case Ident(_) | Select(_, _) =>
320       Typ(pat.tpe.stripAnnots, false)
321     case Alternative(trees) => Or(trees.map(project(_)))
322     case Bind(_, pat) => project(pat)
323     case SeqLiteral(pats, _) => projectSeq(pats)
324     case UnApply(fun, _, pats) =>
325       if (fun.symbol.name == nme.unapplySeq)
326         if (fun.symbol.owner == scalaSeqFactoryClass)
327           projectSeq(pats)
328         else
329           Prod(pat.tpe.stripAnnots, fun.tpe, fun.symbol, projectSeq(pats) :: Nil, irrefutable(fun))
330       else
331         Prod(pat.tpe.stripAnnots, fun.tpe, fun.symbol, pats.map(project), irrefutable(fun))
332     case Typed(pat @ UnApply(_, _, _), _) => project(pat)
333     case Typed(expr, tpt) =>
334       Typ(erase(expr.tpe.stripAnnots), true)
335     case _ =>
336       debug.println(s"unknown pattern: $pat")
337       Empty
338   }
339 
340   /* Erase a type binding according to erasure semantics in pattern matching */
341   def erase(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
342     case tp @ AppliedType(tycon, args) =>
343       if (tycon.isRef(defn.ArrayClass)) tp.derivedAppliedType(tycon, args.map(erase))
344       else tp.derivedAppliedType(tycon, args.map(t => WildcardType))
345     case OrType(tp1, tp2) =>
346       OrType(erase(tp1), erase(tp2))
347     case AndType(tp1, tp2) =>
348       AndType(erase(tp1), erase(tp2))
349     case tp: RefinedType =>
350       tp.derivedRefinedType(erase(tp.parent), tp.refinedName, WildcardType)
351     case _ => tp
352   }
353 
354   /** Space of the pattern: unapplySeq(a, b, c: _*)
355    */
356   def projectSeq(pats: List[Tree]): Space = {
357     if (pats.isEmpty) return Typ(scalaNilType, false)
358 
359     val (items, zero) = if (pats.last.tpe.isRepeatedParam)
360       (pats.init, Typ(scalaListType.appliedTo(pats.last.tpe.argTypes.head), false))
361     else
362       (pats, Typ(scalaNilType, false))
363 
364     items.foldRight[Space](zero) { (pat, acc) =>
365       val consTp = scalaConsType.appliedTo(pats.head.tpe.widen)
366       val unapplySym = consTp.classSymbol.linkedClass.info.member(nme.unapply).symbol
367       val unapplyTp = unapplySym.info.appliedTo(pats.head.tpe.widen)
368       Prod(consTp, unapplyTp, unapplySym, project(pat) :: acc :: Nil, true)
369     }
370   }
371 
372   /** Is `tp1` a subtype of `tp2`?  */
373   def isSubType(tp1: Type, tp2: Type): Boolean = {
374     val res = tp1 <:< tp2
375     debug.println(s"${tp1.show} <:< ${tp2.show} = $res")
376     res
377   }
378 
379   def isEqualType(tp1: Type, tp2: Type): Boolean = tp1 =:= tp2
380 
381   /** Parameter types of the case class type `tp`. Adapted from `unapplyPlan` in patternMatcher  */
382   def signature(unapp: Type, unappSym: Symbol, argLen: Int): List[Type] = {
383     def caseClass = unappSym.owner.linkedClass
384 
385     lazy val caseAccessors = caseClass.caseAccessors.filter(_.is(Method))
386 
387     def isSyntheticScala2Unapply(sym: Symbol) =
388       sym.is(SyntheticCase) && sym.owner.is(Scala2x)
389 
390     val mt @ MethodType(_) = unapp.widen
391 
392     // Case unapply:
393     // 1. return types of constructor fields if the extractor is synthesized for Scala2 case classes & length match
394     // 2. return Nil if unapply returns Boolean  (boolean pattern)
395     // 3. return product selector types if unapply returns a product type (product pattern)
396     // 4. return product selectors of `T` where `def get: T` is a member of the return type of unapply & length match (named-based pattern)
397     // 5. otherwise, return `T` where `def get: T` is a member of the return type of unapply
398     //
399     // Case unapplySeq:
400     // 1. return the type `List[T]` where `T` is the element type of the unapplySeq return type `Seq[T]`
401 
402     val sig =
403       if (isSyntheticScala2Unapply(unappSym) && caseAccessors.length == argLen)
404         caseAccessors.map(_.info.asSeenFrom(mt.paramInfos.head, caseClass).widen)
405       else if (mt.finalResultType.isRef(defn.BooleanClass))
406         List()
407       else {
408         val isUnapplySeq = unappSym.name == nme.unapplySeq
409         if (isProductMatch(mt.finalResultType, argLen) && !isUnapplySeq) {
410           productSelectors(mt.finalResultType).take(argLen)
411             .map(_.info.asSeenFrom(mt.finalResultType, mt.resultType.classSymbol).widen)
412         }
413         else {
414           val resTp = mt.finalResultType.select(nme.get).finalResultType.widen
415           if (isUnapplySeq) scalaListType.appliedTo(resTp.argTypes.head) :: Nil
416           else if (argLen == 0) Nil
417           else if (isProductMatch(resTp, argLen))
418             productSelectors(resTp).map(_.info.asSeenFrom(resTp, resTp.classSymbol).widen)
419           else resTp :: Nil
420         }
421       }
422 
423     debug.println(s"signature of ${unappSym.showFullName} ----> ${sig.map(_.show).mkString(", ")}")
424 
425     sig.map(_.annotatedToRepeated)
426   }
427 
428   /** Decompose a type into subspaces -- assume the type can be decomposed */
429   def decompose(tp: Type): List[Space] = {
430     val children = tp.classSymbol.children
431 
432     debug.println(s"candidates for ${tp.show} : [${children.map(_.show).mkString(", ")}]")
433 
434     tp.dealias match {
435       case AndType(tp1, tp2) =>
436         intersect(Typ(tp1, false), Typ(tp2, false)) match {
437           case Or(spaces) => spaces
438           case Empty => Nil
439           case space => List(space)
440         }
441       case OrType(tp1, tp2) => List(Typ(tp1, true), Typ(tp2, true))
442       case tp if tp.isRef(defn.BooleanClass) =>
443         List(
444           Typ(ConstantType(Constant(true)), true),
445           Typ(ConstantType(Constant(false)), true)
446         )
447       case tp if tp.classSymbol.is(Enum) =>
448         children.map(sym => Typ(sym.termRef, true))
449       case tp =>
450         val parts = children.map { sym =>
451           if (sym.is(ModuleClass))
452             refine(tp, sym.sourceModule)
453           else
454             refine(tp, sym)
455         } filter(_.exists)
456 
457         debug.println(s"${tp.show} decomposes to [${parts.map(_.show).mkString(", ")}]")
458 
459         parts.map(Typ(_, true))
460     }
461   }
462 
463   /** Refine child based on parent
464    *
465    *  In child class definition, we have:
466    *
467    *      class Child[Ts] extends path.Parent[Us] with Es
468    *      object Child extends path.Parent[Us] with Es
469    *      val child = new path.Parent[Us] with Es           // enum values
470    *
471    *  Given a parent type `parent` and a child symbol `child`, we infer the prefix
472    *  and type parameters for the child:
473    *
474    *      prefix.child[Vs] <:< parent
475    *
476    *  where `Vs` are fresh type variables and `prefix` is the symbol prefix with all
477    *  non-module and non-package `ThisType` replaced by fresh type variables.
478    *
479    *  If the subtyping is true, the instantiated type `p.child[Vs]` is
480    *  returned. Otherwise, `NoType` is returned.
481    *
482    */
483   def refine(parent: Type, child: Symbol): Type = {
484     if (child.isTerm && child.is(Case, butNot = Module)) return child.termRef // enum vals always match
485 
486     val childTp = if (child.isTerm) child.termRef else child.typeRef
487 
488     val resTp = instantiate(childTp, parent)(ctx.fresh.setNewTyperState())
489 
490     if (!resTp.exists || !inhabited(resTp)) {
491       debug.println(s"[refine] unqualified child ousted: ${childTp.show} !< ${parent.show}")
492       NoType
493     }
494     else {
495       debug.println(s"$child instantiated ------> $resTp")
496       resTp.dealias
497     }
498   }
499 
500   /** Can this type be inhabited by a value?
501    *
502    *  Check is based on the following facts:
503    *
504    *  - single inheritance of classes
505    *  - final class cannot be extended
506    *  - intersection of a singleton type with another irrelevant type  (patmat/i3574.scala)
507    *
508    */
509   def inhabited(tp: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean = {
510     // convert top-level type shape into "conjunctive normal form"
511     def cnf(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
512       case AndType(OrType(l, r), tp)      =>
513         OrType(cnf(AndType(l, tp)), cnf(AndType(r, tp)))
514       case AndType(tp, o: OrType)         =>
515         cnf(AndType(o, tp))
516       case AndType(l, r)                  =>
517         val l1 = cnf(l)
518         val r1 = cnf(r)
519         if (l1.ne(l) || r1.ne(r)) cnf(AndType(l1, r1))
520         else AndType(l1, r1)
521       case OrType(l, r)                   =>
522         OrType(cnf(l), cnf(r))
523       case tp @ RefinedType(OrType(tp1, tp2), _, _)  =>
524         OrType(
525           cnf(tp.derivedRefinedType(tp1, refinedName = tp.refinedName, refinedInfo = tp.refinedInfo)),
526           cnf(tp.derivedRefinedType(tp2, refinedName = tp.refinedName, refinedInfo = tp.refinedInfo))
527         )
528       case tp: RefinedType                =>
529         val parent1 = cnf(tp.parent)
530         val tp1 = tp.derivedRefinedType(parent1, refinedName = tp.refinedName, refinedInfo = tp.refinedInfo)
531 
532         if (parent1.ne(tp.parent)) cnf(tp1) else tp1
533       case tp: TypeAlias                  =>
534         cnf(tp.alias)
535       case _                              =>
536         tp
537     }
538 
539     def isSingleton(tp: Type): Boolean = tp.dealias match {
540       case AndType(l, r)  => isSingleton(l) || isSingleton(r)
541       case OrType(l, r)   => isSingleton(l) && isSingleton(r)
542       case tp             => tp.isSingleton
543     }
544 
545     def superType(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
546       case tp: TypeProxy     => tp.superType
547       case OrType(tp1, tp2)  => OrType(superType(tp1), superType(tp2))
548       case AndType(tp1, tp2) => AndType(superType(tp1), superType(tp2))
549       case _                 => tp
550     }
551 
552     def recur(tp: Type): Boolean = tp.dealias match {
553       case AndType(tp1, tp2) =>
554         recur(tp1) && recur(tp2) && {
555           val bases1 = tp1.widenDealias.classSymbols
556           val bases2 = tp2.widenDealias.classSymbols
557 
558           debug.println(s"bases of ${tp1.show}: " + bases1)
559           debug.println(s"bases of ${tp2.show}: " + bases2)
560           debug.println(s"${tp1.show} <:< ${tp2.show} : " +  (tp1 <:< tp2))
561           debug.println(s"${tp2.show} <:< ${tp1.show} : " +  (tp2 <:< tp1))
562 
563           val noClassConflict =
564             bases1.forall(sym1 => sym1.is(Trait) || bases2.forall(sym2 => sym2.is(Trait) || sym1.isSubClass(sym2))) ||
565             bases1.forall(sym1 => sym1.is(Trait) || bases2.forall(sym2 => sym2.is(Trait) || sym2.isSubClass(sym1)))
566 
567           debug.println(s"class conflict for ${tp.show}? " + !noClassConflict)
568 
569           noClassConflict &&
570             (!isSingleton(tp1) || tp1 <:< tp2) &&
571             (!isSingleton(tp2) || tp2 <:< tp1) &&
572             (!bases1.exists(_ is Final) || tp1 <:< superType(tp2)) &&
573             (!bases2.exists(_ is Final) || tp2 <:< superType(tp1))
574         }
575       case OrType(tp1, tp2) =>
576         recur(tp1) || recur(tp2)
577       case tp: RefinedType =>
578         recur(tp.parent)
579       case tp: TypeRef =>
580         recur(tp.prefix) && !(tp.classSymbol.is(AbstractFinal))
581       case _ =>
582         true
583     }
584 
585     val res = recur(cnf(tp))
586 
587     debug.println(s"${tp.show} inhabited?  " + res)
588 
589     res
590   }
591 
592   /** Instantiate type `tp1` to be a subtype of `tp2`
593    *
594    *  Return the instantiated type if type parameters and this type
595    *  in `tp1` can be instantiated such that `tp1 <:< tp2`.
596    *
597    *  Otherwise, return NoType.
598    *
599    */
600   def instantiate(tp1: NamedType, tp2: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Type = {
601     // expose abstract type references to their bounds or tvars according to variance
602     class AbstractTypeMap(maximize: Boolean)(implicit ctx: Context) extends TypeMap {
603       def expose(tp: TypeRef): Type = {
604         val lo = this(tp.info.loBound)
605         val hi = this(tp.info.hiBound)
606         val exposed =
607           if (variance == 0)
608             newTypeVar(TypeBounds(lo, hi))
609           else if (variance == 1)
610             if (maximize) hi else lo
611           else
612             if (maximize) lo else hi
613 
614         debug.println(s"$tp exposed to =====> $exposed")
615         exposed
616       }
617 
618       def apply(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
619         case tp: TypeRef if tp.underlying.isInstanceOf[TypeBounds] =>
620           // See tests/patmat/gadt.scala  tests/patmat/exhausting.scala  tests/patmat/t9657.scala
621           expose(tp)
622 
623         case AppliedType(tycon: TypeRef, args) if tycon.underlying.isInstanceOf[TypeBounds] =>
624           val args2 = args.map(this)
625           val lo = this(tycon.info.loBound).applyIfParameterized(args2)
626           val hi = this(tycon.info.hiBound).applyIfParameterized(args2)
627           val exposed =
628             if (variance == 0)
629               newTypeVar(TypeBounds(lo, hi))
630             else if (variance == 1)
631               if (maximize) hi else lo
632             else
633               if (maximize) lo else hi
634 
635           debug.println(s"$tp exposed to =====> $exposed")
636           exposed
637 
638         case _ =>
639           mapOver(tp)
640       }
641     }
642 
643     def minTypeMap(implicit ctx: Context) = new AbstractTypeMap(maximize = false)
644     def maxTypeMap(implicit ctx: Context) = new AbstractTypeMap(maximize = true)
645 
646     // Fix subtype checking for child instantiation,
647     // such that `Foo(Test.this.foo) <:< Foo(Foo.this)`
648     // See tests/patmat/i3938.scala
649     def removeThisType(implicit ctx: Context) = new TypeMap {
650       // is in tvarBounds? Don't create new tvars if true
651       private var tvarBounds: Boolean = false
652       def apply(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
653         case ThisType(tref: TypeRef) if !tref.symbol.isStaticOwner =>
654           if (tref.symbol.is(Module))
655             TermRef(this(tref.prefix), tref.symbol.sourceModule)
656           else if (tvarBounds)
657             this(tref)
658           else {
659             tvarBounds = true
660             newTypeVar(TypeBounds.upper(this(tref)))
661           }
662         case tp => mapOver(tp)
663       }
664     }
665 
666     // replace uninstantiated type vars with WildcardType, check tests/patmat/3333.scala
667     def instUndetMap(implicit ctx: Context) = new TypeMap {
668       def apply(t: Type): Type = t match {
669         case tvar: TypeVar if !tvar.isInstantiated => WildcardType(tvar.origin.underlying.bounds)
670         case _ => mapOver(t)
671       }
672     }
673 
674     val force = new ForceDegree.Value(
675       tvar => !(ctx.typerState.constraint.entry(tvar.origin) eq tvar.origin.underlying),
676       minimizeAll = false
677     )
678 
679     val tvars = tp1.typeParams.map { tparam => newTypeVar(tparam.paramInfo.bounds) }
680     val protoTp1 = removeThisType.apply(tp1).appliedTo(tvars)
681 
682     // If parent contains a reference to an abstract type, then we should
683     // refine subtype checking to eliminate abstract types according to
684     // variance. As this logic is only needed in exhaustivity check,
685     // we manually patch subtyping check instead of changing TypeComparer.
686     // See tests/patmat/i3645b.scala
687     def parentQualify = tp1.widen.classSymbol.info.parents.exists { parent =>
688       implicit val ictx = ctx.fresh.setNewTyperState()
689       parent.argInfos.nonEmpty && minTypeMap.apply(parent) <:< maxTypeMap.apply(tp2)
690     }
691 
692     if (protoTp1 <:< tp2) {
693       if (isFullyDefined(protoTp1, force)) protoTp1
694       else instUndetMap.apply(protoTp1)
695     }
696     else {
697       val protoTp2 = maxTypeMap.apply(tp2)
698       if (protoTp1 <:< protoTp2 || parentQualify) {
699         if (isFullyDefined(AndType(protoTp1, protoTp2), force)) protoTp1
700         else instUndetMap.apply(protoTp1)
701       }
702       else {
703         debug.println(s"$protoTp1 <:< $protoTp2 = false")
704         NoType
705       }
706     }
707   }
708 
709   /** Abstract sealed types, or-types, Boolean and Java enums can be decomposed */
710   def canDecompose(tp: Type): Boolean = {
711     val dealiasedTp = tp.dealias
712     val res =
713       (tp.classSymbol.is(Sealed) &&
714         tp.classSymbol.is(AbstractOrTrait) &&
715         tp.classSymbol.children.nonEmpty ) ||
716       dealiasedTp.isInstanceOf[OrType] ||
717       (dealiasedTp.isInstanceOf[AndType] && {
718         val and = dealiasedTp.asInstanceOf[AndType]
719         canDecompose(and.tp1) || canDecompose(and.tp2)
720       }) ||
721       tp.isRef(defn.BooleanClass) ||
722       tp.classSymbol.is(allOf(Enum, Sealed))  // Enum value doesn't have Sealed flag
723 
724     debug.println(s"decomposable: ${tp.show} = $res")
725 
726     res
727   }
728 
729   /** Show friendly type name with current scope in mind
730    *
731    *  E.g.    C.this.B     -->  B     if current owner is C
732    *          C.this.x.T   -->  x.T   if current owner is C
733    *          X[T]         -->  X
734    *          C            -->  C     if current owner is C !!!
735    *
736    */
737   def showType(tp: Type): String = {
738     val enclosingCls = ctx.owner.enclosingClass
739 
740     def isOmittable(sym: Symbol) =
741       sym.isEffectiveRoot || sym.isAnonymousClass || sym.name.isReplWrapperName ||
742         ctx.definitions.UnqualifiedOwnerTypes.exists(_.symbol == sym) ||
743         sym.showFullName.startsWith("scala.") ||
744         sym == enclosingCls || sym == enclosingCls.sourceModule
745 
746     def refinePrefix(tp: Type): String = tp match {
747       case NoPrefix => ""
748       case tp: NamedType if isOmittable(tp.symbol) => ""
749       case tp: ThisType => refinePrefix(tp.tref)
750       case tp: RefinedType => refinePrefix(tp.parent)
751       case tp: NamedType => tp.name.show.stripSuffix("$")
752       case tp: TypeVar => refinePrefix(tp.instanceOpt)
753       case _ => tp.show
754     }
755 
756     def refine(tp: Type): String = tp match {
757       case tp: RefinedType => refine(tp.parent)
758       case tp: AppliedType => refine(tp.typeConstructor)
759       case tp: ThisType => refine(tp.tref)
760       case tp: NamedType =>
761         val pre = refinePrefix(tp.prefix)
762         if (tp.name == tpnme.higherKinds) pre
763         else if (pre.isEmpty) tp.name.show.stripSuffix("$")
764         else pre + "." + tp.name.show.stripSuffix("$")
765       case _ => tp.show.stripSuffix("$")
766     }
767 
768     val text = tp.stripAnnots match {
769       case tp: OrType => showType(tp.tp1) + " | " + showType(tp.tp2)
770       case tp => refine(tp)
771     }
772 
773     if (text.isEmpty) enclosingCls.show.stripSuffix("$")
774     else text
775   }
776 
777   /** Whether the counterexample is satisfiable. The space is flattened and non-empty. */
778   def satisfiable(sp: Space): Boolean = {
779     def impossible: Nothing = throw new AssertionError("`satisfiable` only accepts flattened space.")
780 
781     def genConstraint(space: Space): List[(Type, Type)] = space match {
782       case Prod(tp, unappTp, unappSym, ss, _) =>
783         val tps = signature(unappTp, unappSym, ss.length)
784         ss.zip(tps).flatMap {
785           case (sp : Prod, tp) => sp.tp -> tp :: genConstraint(sp)
786           case (Typ(tp1, _), tp2) => tp1 -> tp2 :: Nil
787           case _ => impossible
788         }
789       case Typ(_, _) => Nil
790       case _ => impossible
791     }
792 
793     def checkConstraint(constrs: List[(Type, Type)])(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean = {
794       val tvarMap = collection.mutable.Map.empty[Symbol, TypeVar]
795       val typeParamMap = new TypeMap() {
796         override def apply(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
797           case tref: TypeRef if tref.symbol.is(TypeParam) =>
798             tvarMap.getOrElseUpdate(tref.symbol, newTypeVar(tref.underlying.bounds))
799           case tp => mapOver(tp)
800         }
801       }
802 
803       constrs.forall { case (tp1, tp2) => typeParamMap(tp1) <:< typeParamMap(tp2) }
804     }
805 
806     checkConstraint(genConstraint(sp))(ctx.fresh.setNewTyperState())
807   }
808 
809   /** Display spaces */
810   def show(s: Space): String = {
811     def params(tp: Type): List[Type] = tp.classSymbol.primaryConstructor.info.firstParamTypes
812 
813     /** does the companion object of the given symbol have custom unapply */
814     def hasCustomUnapply(sym: Symbol): Boolean = {
815       val companion = sym.companionModule
816       companion.findMember(nme.unapply, NoPrefix, excluded = Synthetic).exists ||
817         companion.findMember(nme.unapplySeq, NoPrefix, excluded = Synthetic).exists
818     }
819 
820     def doShow(s: Space, mergeList: Boolean = false): String = s match {
821       case Empty => ""
822       case Typ(c: ConstantType, _) => c.value.show
823       case Typ(tp: TermRef, _) => tp.symbol.showName
824       case Typ(tp, decomposed) =>
825         val sym = tp.widen.classSymbol
826 
827         if (ctx.definitions.isTupleType(tp))
828           params(tp).map(_ => "_").mkString("(", ", ", ")")
829         else if (scalaListType.isRef(sym))
830           if (mergeList) "_: _*" else "_: List"
831         else if (scalaConsType.isRef(sym))
832           if (mergeList) "_, _: _*"  else "List(_, _: _*)"
833         else if (tp.classSymbol.is(CaseClass) && !hasCustomUnapply(tp.classSymbol))
834         // use constructor syntax for case class
835           showType(tp) + params(tp).map(_ => "_").mkString("(", ", ", ")")
836         else if (decomposed) "_: " + showType(tp)
837         else "_"
838       case Prod(tp, fun, sym, params, _) =>
839         if (ctx.definitions.isTupleType(tp))
840           "(" + params.map(doShow(_)).mkString(", ") + ")"
841         else if (tp.isRef(scalaConsType.symbol))
842           if (mergeList) params.map(doShow(_, mergeList)).mkString(", ")
843           else params.map(doShow(_, true)).filter(_ != "Nil").mkString("List(", ", ", ")")
844         else
845           showType(sym.owner.typeRef) + params.map(doShow(_)).mkString("(", ", ", ")")
846       case Or(_) =>
847         throw new Exception("incorrect flatten result " + s)
848     }
849 
850     flatten(s).map(doShow(_, false)).distinct.mkString(", ")
851   }
852 
853   def checkable(tree: Match): Boolean = {
854     // Possible to check everything, but be compatible with scalac by default
855     def isCheckable(tp: Type): Boolean =
856       !tp.hasAnnotation(defn.UncheckedAnnot) && {
857         val tpw = tp.widen.dealias
858         ctx.settings.YcheckAllPatmat.value ||
859         tpw.typeSymbol.is(Sealed) ||
860         tpw.isInstanceOf[OrType] ||
861         (tpw.isInstanceOf[AndType] && {
862           val and = tpw.asInstanceOf[AndType]
863           isCheckable(and.tp1) || isCheckable(and.tp2)
864         }) ||
865         tpw.isRef(defn.BooleanClass) ||
866         tpw.typeSymbol.is(Enum) ||
867         canDecompose(tpw) ||
868         (defn.isTupleType(tpw) && tpw.argInfos.exists(isCheckable(_)))
869       }
870 
871     val Match(sel, cases) = tree
872     val res = isCheckable(sel.tpe)
873     debug.println(s"checkable: ${sel.show} = $res")
874     res
875   }
876 
877   /** Whehter counter-examples should be further checked? True for GADTs. */
878   def shouldCheckExamples(tp: Type): Boolean = {
879     new TypeAccumulator[Boolean] {
880       override def apply(b: Boolean, tp: Type): Boolean = tp match {
881         case tref: TypeRef if tref.symbol.is(TypeParam) && variance != 1 => true
882         case tp => b || foldOver(b, tp)
883       }
884     }.apply(false, tp)
885   }
886 
887   def checkExhaustivity(_match: Match): Unit = {
888     val Match(sel, cases) = _match
889     val selTyp = sel.tpe.widen.dealias
890 
891 
892     val patternSpace = cases.map({ x =>
893       val space = project(x.pat)
894       debug.println(s"${x.pat.show} ====> ${show(space)}")
895       space
896     }).reduce((a, b) => Or(List(a, b)))
897 
898     val checkGADTSAT = shouldCheckExamples(selTyp)
899 
900     val uncovered =
901       flatten(simplify(minus(Typ(selTyp, true), patternSpace), aggressive = true))
902         .filter(s => s != Empty && (!checkGADTSAT || satisfiable(s)))
903 
904     if (uncovered.nonEmpty)
905       ctx.warning(PatternMatchExhaustivity(show(Or(uncovered))), sel.pos)
906   }
907 
908   def checkRedundancy(_match: Match): Unit = {
909     val Match(sel, cases) = _match
910     // ignore selector type for now
911     val selTyp = sel.tpe.widen.dealias
912 
913     (0 until cases.length).foreach { i =>
914       // in redundancy check, take guard as false in order to soundly approximate
915       val prevs =
916         if (i == 0)
917           Empty
918         else
919           cases.take(i).map { x =>
920             if (x.guard.isEmpty) project(x.pat)
921             else Empty
922           }.reduce((a, b) => Or(List(a, b)))
923 
924       val curr = project(cases(i).pat)
925 
926       debug.println(s"---------------reachable? ${show(curr)}")
927       debug.println(s"prev: ${show(prevs)}")
928 
929       if (isSubspace(intersect(curr, Typ(selTyp, false)), prevs)) {
930         ctx.warning(MatchCaseUnreachable(), cases(i).body.pos)
931       }
932     }
933   }
934 }
